    17	type Model struct {
    18	        ctx                *context.ProgramContext
    19	        textArea           textarea.Model
    20	        inputHelp          help.Model
    21	        prompt             string
    22	        autocomplete       *autocomplete.Model
    23	        autocompleteSource dataautocomplete.Source
    24	}
    25	
    26	var inputKeys = []key.Binding{
    27	        key.NewBinding(key.WithKeys("ctrl+d"), key.WithHelp("Ctrl+d", "submit")),
    28	        key.NewBinding(key.WithKeys("ctrl+c", "esc"), key.WithHelp("Ctrl+c/esc", "cancel")),
    29	        autocomplete.ToggleSuggestions,
    30	}
    31	
    32	func NewModel(ctx *context.ProgramContext) Model {
    33	        ta := textarea.New()
    34	        ta.ShowLineNumbers = true
    35	        ta.Prompt = ""
    36	        ta.CharLimit = 65536
    37	        base := lipgloss.NewStyle()
    38	        ta.SetStyles(textarea.Styles{
    39	                Focused: textarea.StyleState{
    40	                        Base:       base,
    41	                        Text:       base.Foreground(ctx.Theme.PrimaryText),
    42	                        LineNumber: base.Foreground(ctx.Theme.FaintText),
    43	                        CursorLine: base.Background(ctx.Theme.FaintBorder).
    44	                                Foreground(ctx.Theme.PrimaryText),
    45	                        CursorLineNumber: base.Foreground(ctx.Theme.SecondaryText),
    46	                        Placeholder:      base.Foreground(ctx.Theme.FaintText),
    47	                        EndOfBuffer:      base.Foreground(ctx.Theme.FaintText),
    48	                },
    49	        })
    50	        ta.Focus()
    51	
    52	        h := help.New()
    53	        h.Styles = ctx.Styles.Help.BubbleStyles
    54	        return Model{
    55	                ctx:       ctx,
    56	                textArea:  ta,
    57	                inputHelp: h,
    58	                prompt:    "",
    59	        }
    60	}

    62	func (m *Model) SetAutocomplete(ac *autocomplete.Model) {
    63	        m.autocomplete = ac
    64	}
    65	
    66	func (m *Model) SetAutocompleteSource(src dataautocomplete.Source) {
    67	        m.autocompleteSource = src
    68	}
    69	
    70	func (m Model) CurrentAutocompleteContext() dataautocomplete.Context {
    71	        if m.autocompleteSource == nil {
    72	                return dataautocomplete.Context{}
    73	        }
    74	
    75	        return m.autocompleteSource.ExtractContext(m.textArea.Value(), m.CursorPosition())
    76	}
    77	
    78	func (m Model) AutocompleteItemsToExclude() []string {
    79	        if m.autocompleteSource == nil {
    80	                return nil
    81	        }
    82	
    83	        return m.autocompleteSource.ItemsToExclude(m.textArea.Value(), m.CursorPosition())
    84	}
    85	
    86	func (m Model) Update(msg tea.Msg) (Model, tea.Cmd) {
    87	        var cmd tea.Cmd
    88	
    89	        switch msg := msg.(type) {
    90	        case tea.KeyMsg:
    91	                // Allow toggling suggestions at any time
    92	                if m.autocomplete != nil && key.Matches(msg, autocomplete.ToggleSuggestions) {
    93	                        if m.autocomplete.IsVisible() {
    94	                                m.autocomplete.Suppress()
    95	                                return m, nil
    96	                        }
    97	
    98	                        m.autocomplete.Unsuppress()
    99	                        currentContext := m.CurrentAutocompleteContext()
   100	                        m.autocomplete.Show(currentContext.Content, m.AutocompleteItemsToExclude())
   101	                        return m, nil
   102	                }
   103	
   104	                // Allow navigation/selection even if the popup is hidden (as long as there are filtered results)
   105	                if m.autocomplete != nil &&
   106	                        (m.autocomplete.IsVisible() || m.autocomplete.HasSuggestions()) {
   107	                        switch {
   108	                        case key.Matches(msg, autocomplete.PrevKey):
   109	                                m.autocomplete.Prev()
   110	                                return m, nil
   111	                        case key.Matches(msg, autocomplete.NextKey):
   112	                                m.autocomplete.Next()
   113	                                return m, nil
   114	                        case key.Matches(msg, autocomplete.SelectKey):
   115	                                selected := m.autocomplete.Selected()
   116	                                if selected != "" && m.autocompleteSource != nil {
   117	                                        currentValue := m.textArea.Value()
   118	                                        currentContext := m.CurrentAutocompleteContext()
   119	                                        newValue, newCursorPos := m.autocompleteSource.InsertSuggestion(
   120	                                                currentValue,
   121	                                                selected,
   122	                                                currentContext.Start,
   123	                                                currentContext.End,
   124	                                        )
   125	                                        m.textArea.SetValue(newValue)
   126	                                        m.textArea.SetCursorColumn(newCursorPos)
   127	                                        // Refresh autocomplete to exclude the newly-added item
   128	                                        if m.AutocompleteItemsToExclude() != nil {
   129	                                                newContext := m.CurrentAutocompleteContext()
   130	                                                m.autocomplete.Show(newContext.Content, m.AutocompleteItemsToExclude())
   131	                                        }
   132	                                }
   133	                                return m, nil
   134	                        }
   135	                }
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        m.textArea, cmd = m.textArea.Update(msg)
   139	        return m, cmd
   140	}
   141	
   142	func (m Model) View() string {
   143	        return lipgloss.NewStyle().
   144	                BorderTop(true).
   145	                BorderStyle(lipgloss.NormalBorder()).
   146	                BorderForeground(m.ctx.Theme.SecondaryBorder).
   147	                MarginTop(1).
   148	                Render(
   149	                        lipgloss.JoinVertical(
   150	                                lipgloss.Left,
   151	                                fmt.Sprintf("%s\n", m.prompt),
   152	                                m.textArea.View(),
   153	                                lipgloss.NewStyle().
   154	                                        MarginTop(1).
   155	                                        Render(m.inputHelp.ShortHelpView(inputKeys)),
   156	                        ),
   157	                )
   158	}
   159	
   160	func (m Model) ViewWithAutocomplete() string {
   161	        autocompleteView := ""
   162	        if m.autocomplete != nil && m.autocomplete.IsVisible() {
   163	                autocompleteView = m.autocomplete.View()
   164	        }
   165	
   166	        return lipgloss.NewStyle().
   167	                BorderTop(true).
   168	                BorderStyle(lipgloss.NormalBorder()).
   169	                BorderForeground(m.ctx.Theme.SecondaryBorder).
   170	                MarginTop(1).
   171	                Render(
   172	                        lipgloss.JoinVertical(
   173	                                lipgloss.Left,
   174	                                fmt.Sprintf("%s\n", m.prompt),
   175	                                m.textArea.View(),
   176	                                autocompleteView,
   177	                                lipgloss.NewStyle().
   178	                                        MarginTop(1).
   179	                                        Render(m.inputHelp.ShortHelpView(inputKeys)),
   180	                        ),
   181	                )
   182	}

   220	
   221	// CursorPosition returns the cursor position within the current logical line
   222	// in runes. This correctly handles multi-byte Unicode characters since the
   223	// textarea internally uses rune-based positioning via [][]rune.
   224	//
   225	// Use this for single-line input contexts like comma-separated labels.
   226	// For multi-line contexts (e.g., @mentions in comments), use GetAbsoluteCursorPosition.
   227	func (m *Model) CursorPosition() int {
   228	        lineInfo := m.textArea.LineInfo()
   229	        return lineInfo.StartColumn + lineInfo.ColumnOffset
   230	}

    46	func NewModel(ctx *context.ProgramContext) Model {
    47	        c := carousel.New(
    48	                carousel.WithItems(tabs),
    49	                carousel.WithWidth(ctx.MainContentWidth),
    50	        )
    51

    53	                pr:       nil,

    55	                editor:   detailedit.New(ctx),
    56	        }
    57	}
    58	
    59	func (m Model) Update(msg tea.Msg) (Model, tea.Cmd) {
    60	        editor, cmd, submit, handled := m.editor.Update(msg)
    61	        m.editor = editor
    62	
    63	        if submit != nil {
    64	                if m.pr == nil {
    65	                        return m, nil
    66	                }
    67	
    68	                sid := tasks.SectionIdentifier{Id: m.sectionId, Type: prssection.SectionType}
    69	
    70	                switch submit.Mode {
    71	                case detailedit.ModeComment:
    72	                        if len(strings.TrimSpace(submit.Value)) != 0 {
    73	                                return m, tasks.CommentOnPR(m.ctx, sid, m.pr.Data.Primary, submit.Value)
    74	                        }
    75	                        return m, nil
    76	
    77	                case detailedit.ModeApprove:
    78	                        comment := ""
    79	                        if len(strings.TrimSpace(submit.Value)) != 0 {
    80	                                comment = submit.Value
    81	                        }
    82	                        return m, tasks.ApprovePR(m.ctx, sid, m.pr.Data.Primary, comment)
    83	
    84	                case detailedit.ModeAssign:
    85	                        usernames := dataautocomplete.AllWords(submit.Value)
    86	                        if len(usernames) > 0 {
    87	                                return m, tasks.AssignPR(m.ctx, sid, m.pr.Data.Primary, usernames)
    88	                        }
    89	                        return m, nil
    90	
    91	                case detailedit.ModeUnassign:
    92	                        usernames := dataautocomplete.AllWords(submit.Value)
    93	                        if len(usernames) > 0 {
    94	                                return m, tasks.UnassignPR(m.ctx, sid, m.pr.Data.Primary, usernames)
    95	                        }
    96	                        return m, nil
    97	
    98	                case detailedit.ModeLabel:
    99	                        labels := dataautocomplete.CurrentLabels(submit.Value)
   100	                        if len(labels) > 0 || len(m.pr.Data.Primary.Labels.Nodes) > 0 {
   101	                                return m, m.label(labels)
   102	                        }
   103	                        return m, nil
   104	                }
   105	        }
   106	        if handled {
   107	                return m, cmd
   108	        }
   109	
   110	        if keyMsg, ok := msg.(tea.KeyMsg); ok {
   111	                switch {
   112	                case key.Matches(keyMsg, keys.PRKeys.PrevSidebarTab):
   113	                        m.carousel.MoveLeft()
   114	                case key.Matches(keyMsg, keys.PRKeys.NextSidebarTab):
   115	                        m.carousel.MoveRight()
   116	                }
   117	        }
   118	
   119	        return m, cmd
   120	}

    50

    54	                }

    62	                        }
    63	                        return m, nil, nil
    64

    69	                        }

    75	                                return m, tasks.UnassignIssue(m.ctx, sid, m.issue.Data, usernames), nil
    76	                        }
    77	                        return m, nil, nil
    78

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
cat > /testbed/mnt_tmp/repro_paste.go <<'GOEOF'
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"os"

	tea "charm.land/bubbletea/v2"

	"github.com/dlvhdr/gh-dash/v4/internal/config"
	dataautocomplete "github.com/dlvhdr/gh-dash/v4/internal/data/autocomplete"
	"github.com/dlvhdr/gh-dash/v4/internal/tui/components/detailedit"
	"github.com/dlvhdr/gh-dash/v4/internal/tui/context"
	"github.com/dlvhdr/gh-dash/v4/internal/tui/theme"
)

func main() {
	cfg, err := config.ParseConfig(config.Location{ConfigFlag: "../internal/config/testdata/test-config.yml", SkipGlobalConfig: true})
	if err != nil { panic(err) }
	thm := theme.ParseTheme(&cfg)
	ctx := &context.ProgramContext{Config: &cfg, Theme: thm, Styles: context.InitStyles(thm)}

	c := detailedit.New(ctx)
	c, _ = c.Enter(detailedit.EnterOptions{
		Mode: detailedit.ModeComment,
		Prompt: "comment",
		Source: dataautocomplete.UserMentionSource{},
		Repo: detailedit.RepoRef{NameWithOwner: "owner/repo", Owner: "owner", Name: "repo"},
		SuggestionKind: detailedit.SuggestionNone,
		EnterFetch: detailedit.FetchNone,
	})

	paste := "this should paste into gh-dash"
	var submit *detailedit.Submit
	var handled bool
	c, _, submit, handled = c.Update(tea.PasteMsg{Content: paste})
	if !handled {
		fmt.Fprintln(os.Stderr, "paste was not handled by active detail editor")
		os.Exit(1)
	}
	c, _, submit, handled = c.Update(tea.KeyPressMsg{Text: "ctrl+d"})
	if submit == nil {
		fmt.Fprintf(os.Stderr, "submit missing (handled=%v)\n", handled)
		os.Exit(1)
	}
	if submit.Value != paste {
		fmt.Fprintf(os.Stderr, "paste failed: got %q want %q\n", submit.Value, paste)
		os.Exit(1)
	}
	fmt.Println("paste reproduced/fixed")
}
GOEOF
trap 'rm -f /testbed/mnt_tmp/repro_paste.go' EXIT
cd /testbed/mnt_tmp
go run ./repro_paste.go
EOF

func (c Controller) updateInput(msg tea.Msg) (Controller, tea.Cmd) {
	var previousContext dataautocomplete.Context
	if c.usesAutocomplete() {
		previousContext = c.inputBox.CurrentAutocompleteContext()
	}

	var cmd tea.Cmd
	c.inputBox, cmd = c.inputBox.Update(msg)

	if c.usesAutocomplete() {
		currentContext := c.inputBox.CurrentAutocompleteContext()
		if currentContext != previousContext {
			if c.hideOnEmpty && currentContext == (dataautocomplete.Context{}) {
				c.ac.Hide()
			} else {
				c.ac.Show(currentContext.Content, c.inputBox.AutocompleteItemsToExclude())
			}
		}
	}

	return c, cmd
}

		previousContext = c.inputBox.CurrentAutocompleteContext()
	}

	var cmd tea.Cmd
	c.inputBox, cmd = c.inputBox.Update(msg)

	if c.usesAutocomplete() {
		currentContext := c.inputBox.CurrentAutocompleteContext()
		if currentContext != previousContext {

func (c *Controller) clearRelevantCache() {
	switch c.suggestionKind {
	case SuggestionUsers:
		if c.repo.NameWithOwner != "" {
			data.ClearRepoUserCache(c.repo.NameWithOwner)
		}
	case SuggestionLabels:
		if c.repo.NameWithOwner != "" {

		}
	}

   160	
   161	func (m Model) Init() tea.Cmd {
   162	        return tea.Batch(tea.RequestBackgroundColor, m.initScreen)
   163	}
   164	
   165	func (m Model) Update(msg tea.Msg) (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
   166	        var (
   167	                cmd             tea.Cmd
   168	                tabsCmd         tea.Cmd
   169	                sidebarCmd      tea.Cmd
   170	                prViewCmd       tea.Cmd
   171	                issueSidebarCmd tea.Cmd
   172	                footerCmd       tea.Cmd
   173	                cmds            []tea.Cmd
   174	                currSection     = m.getCurrSection()
   175	                currRowData     = m.getCurrRowData()
   176	        )
   177	
   178	        switch msg := msg.(type) {
   179	        case tea.KeyMsg:
   180	                log.Info("Key pressed", "key", msg.String())
   181	                m.ctx.Error = nil
   182	
   183	                if currSection != nil && (currSection.IsSearchFocused() ||
   184	                        currSection.IsPromptConfirmationFocused()) {
   185	                        cmd = m.updateSection(currSection.GetId(), currSection.GetType(), msg)
   186	                        return m, cmd
   187	                }
   188	
   189	                if m.prView.IsTextInputBoxFocused() {
   190	                        m.prView, cmd = m.prView.Update(msg)
   191	                        m.syncSidebar()
   192	                        return m, cmd
   193	                }
   194	
   195	                if m.issueSidebar.IsTextInputBoxFocused() {
   196	                        m.issueSidebar, cmd, _ = m.issueSidebar.Update(msg)
   197	                        m.syncSidebar()
   198	                        return m, cmd
   199	                }
   200	
   201	                if m.footer.ShowConfirmQuit && (msg.String() == "y" || msg.String() == "enter") {
   202	                        return m, tea.Quit
   203	                } else if m.footer.ShowConfirmQuit {
   204	                        m.footer.SetShowConfirmQuit(false)
   205	                        return m, nil
   206	                }
   207	
   208	                // Handle notification PR/Issue action confirmation
   209	                if m.notificationView.HasPendingAction() {
   210	                        var action string
   211	                        m.notificationView, action = m.notificationView.Update(msg)
   212	                        m.footer.SetLeftSection("")
   213	                        if action != "" {
   214	                                return m, m.executeNotificationAction(action)
   215	                        }
   216	                        return m, nil
   217	                }
   218	
   219	                switch {
   220	                case m.isUserDefinedKeybinding(msg):
   221	                        cmd = m.executeKeybinding(msg.String())
   222	                        return m, cmd

+func (c Controller) updateInput(msg tea.Msg) (Controller, tea.Cmd) {
+	var previousContext dataautocomplete.Context
+	if c.usesAutocomplete() {
+		previousContext = c.inputBox.CurrentAutocompleteContext()
+	}
+
+	var cmd tea.Cmd
+	c.inputBox, cmd = c.inputBox.Update(msg)
+
+	if c.usesAutocomplete() {
+		currentContext := c.inputBox.CurrentAutocompleteContext()
+		if currentContext != previousContext {
+			if c.hideOnEmpty && currentContext == (dataautocomplete.Context{}) {
+				c.ac.Hide()
+			} else {
+				c.ac.Show(currentContext.Content, c.inputBox.AutocompleteItemsToExclude())
+			}
+		}
+	}
+
+	return c, cmd
